 What to do to strengthen the Manipur Chakra? - Wear a red robe at midnight - First pay obeisance to your Guru - Light a lamp in front of Maa Durga, and offer red flowers to her - Then meditate on the commandment chakra - After meditation Pray to your Guru to strengthen the Manipur Chakra, chanting the mantra of Aishwarya Akshay and Mukti Mukti on the third day of Mahamantri Navaratri, associated with the third form of Devi
